libgcj-devel-4.4.7-3.el6 RPM for x86_64

From CentOS 6.4 for x86_64 / Packages

Name: libgcj-devel Distribution: Unknown
Version: 4.4.7 Vendor: CentOS
Release: 3.el6 Build date: Thu Feb 21 18:16:26 2013
Group: Development/Languages Build host: c6b9.bsys.dev.centos.org
Size: 6276360 Source RPM: gcc-4.4.7-3.el6.src.rpm
Packager: CentOS BuildSystem <http://bugs.centos.org>
Url: http://gcc.gnu.org
Summary: Libraries for Java development using GCC
 
The Java(tm) static libraries and C header files. You will need this
package to compile your Java programs using the GCC Java compiler (gcj).

Provides

  • libgcj-devel
  • libgcj-devel(x86-64)

Requires

  • libgcj(x86-64) = 4.4.7-3.el6
  • zlib-devel(x86-64)
  • /bin/awk <=
  • rpmlib(VersionedDependencies) <= 3.0.3-1
  • rpmlib(FileDigests) < 4.6.0-1
  • rpmlib(PayloadFilesHavePrefix) < 4.0-1
  • rpmlib(CompressedFileNames) <= 3.0.4-1
  • rpmlib(PayloadIsXz) < 5.2-1

License

GPLv3+ and GPLv3+ with exceptions and GPLv2+ with exceptions
